    56	/**
    57	 * Modifies the passed in Next.js configuration with automatic build-time instrumentation and source map upload.
    58	 *
    59	 * @param nextConfig A Next.js configuration object, as usually exported in `next.config.js` or `next.config.mjs`.
    60	 * @param sentryBuildOptions Additional options to configure instrumentation and
    61	 * @returns The modified config to be exported
    62	 */
    63	export function withSentryConfig<C>(nextConfig?: C, sentryBuildOptions: SentryBuildOptions = {}): C {
    64	  const castNextConfig = (nextConfig as NextConfig) || {};
    65	  if (typeof castNextConfig === 'function') {
    66	    return function (this: unknown, ...webpackConfigFunctionArgs: unknown[]): ReturnType<NextConfigFunction> {
    67	      const maybePromiseNextConfig: ReturnType<typeof castNextConfig> = castNextConfig.apply(
    68	        this,
    69	        webpackConfigFunctionArgs,
    70	      );
    71	
    72	      if (isThenable(maybePromiseNextConfig)) {
    73	        return maybePromiseNextConfig.then(promiseResultNextConfig => {
    74	          return getFinalConfigObject(promiseResultNextConfig, sentryBuildOptions);
    75	        });
    76	      }
    77	
    78	      return getFinalConfigObject(maybePromiseNextConfig, sentryBuildOptions);
    79	    } as C;
    80	  } else {
    81	    return getFinalConfigObject(castNextConfig, sentryBuildOptions) as C;
    82	  }
    83	}
    84	
    85	/**
    86	 * Generates a random tunnel route path that's less likely to be blocked by ad-blockers
    87	 */
    88	function generateRandomTunnelRoute(): string {
    89	  // Generate a random 8-character alphanumeric string
    90	  const randomString = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10);
    91	  return `/${randomString}`;
    92	}

     2	import * as chalk from 'chalk';
     3	import * as path from 'path';
     4	import type { RouteManifest } from '../manifest/types';
     5	import type { NextConfigObject, TurbopackOptions, TurbopackRuleConfigItemOrShortcut } from '../types';
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Construct a Turbopack config object from a Next.js config object and a Turbopack options object.
     9	 *
    10	 * @param userNextConfig - The Next.js config object.
    11	 * @param turbopackOptions - The Turbopack options object.
    12	 * @returns The Turbopack config object.
    13	 */
    14	export function constructTurbopackConfig({
    15	  userNextConfig,
    16	  routeManifest,
    17	}: {
    18	  userNextConfig: NextConfigObject;
    19	  routeManifest?: RouteManifest;
    20	}): TurbopackOptions {
    21	  const newConfig: TurbopackOptions = {
    22	    ...userNextConfig.turbopack,
    23	  };
    24	
    25	  if (routeManifest) {
    26	    newConfig.rules = safelyAddTurbopackRule(newConfig.rules, {
    27	      matcher: '**/instrumentation-client.*',
    28	      rule: {
    29	        loaders: [
    30	          {
    31	            loader: path.resolve(__dirname, '..', 'loaders', 'valueInjectionLoader.js'),
    32	            options: {
    33	              values: {
    34	                _sentryRouteManifest: JSON.stringify(routeManifest),
    35	              },
    36	            },
    37	          },
    38	        ],
    39	      },
    40	    });
    41	  }
    42	
    43	  return newConfig;
    44	}
    45	
    46	/**
    47	 * Safely add a Turbopack rule to the existing rules.
    48	 *
    49	 * @param existingRules - The existing rules.
    50	 * @param matcher - The matcher for the rule.
    51	 * @param rule - The rule to add.
    52	 * @returns The updated rules object.
    53	 */
    54	export function safelyAddTurbopackRule(
    55	  existingRules: TurbopackOptions['rules'],
    56	  { matcher, rule }: { matcher: string; rule: TurbopackRuleConfigItemOrShortcut },
    57	): TurbopackOptions['rules'] {
    58	  if (!existingRules) {
    59	    return {
    60	      [matcher]: rule,
    61	    };
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  // If the rule already exists, we don't want to mess with it.
    65	  if (existingRules[matcher]) {
    66	    logger.info(
    67	      `${chalk.cyan(
    68	        'info',
    69	      )} - Turbopack rule already exists for ${matcher}. Please remove it from your Next.js config in order for Sentry to work properly.`,
    70	    );
    71	    return existingRules;
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  return {
    75	    ...existingRules,
    76	    [matcher]: rule,
    77	  };
    78	}

Now I understand the issue. Looking at the code in `/testbed/packages/nextjs/src/config/withSentryConfig.ts`, I can see the problem:

1. When Turbopack is enabled (`process.env.TURBOPACK` is truthy), Sentry still sets the `webpack` property to `undefined` (line 314-316) instead of not setting it at all.

2. Even though it's set to `undefined`, Next.js 15.3 detects that the `webpack` property is present in the configuration and shows a warning that "Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not".

Let me check what the current logic is doing:

The current logic:
```typescript
webpack: !isTurbopack
  ? constructWebpackConfigFunction(...)
  : undefined,
```

This sets `webpack: undefined` when Turbopack is enabled. However, Next.js sees this as "Webpack is configured" because the property exists.

The fix should be to only set the `webpack` property when Turbopack is NOT enabled, and omit it entirely when Turbopack IS enabled.

Let me also check if there are any tests to understand the expected behavior:

2026-01-10 06:00:01,220 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Based on my analysis, the issue is clear. When using Next.js 15.3 with Turbopack, Sentry's configuration is setting the `webpack` property to `undefined` when Turbopack is enabled. However, Next.js 15.3 detects that the `webpack` property exists (even as `undefined`) and shows a warning that "Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not".

The fix is to only include the `webpack` property in the configuration when Turbopack is NOT enabled, and omit it entirely when Turbopack IS enabled.

Let me implement the fix:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/packages/nextjs/src/config/withSentryConfig.ts   --old_str '  return {
    ...incomingUserNextConfigObject,
    ...(nextMajor && nextMajor >= 15
      ? {
          serverExternalPackages: [
            ...(incomingUserNextConfigObject.serverExternalPackages || []),
            ...DEFAULT_SERVER_EXTERNAL_PACKAGES,
          ],
        }
      : {
          experimental: {
            ...incomingUserNextConfigObject.experimental,
            serverComponentsExternalPackages: [
              ...(incomingUserNextConfigObject.experimental?.serverComponentsExternalPackages || []),
              ...DEFAULT_SERVER_EXTERNAL_PACKAGES,
            ],
          },
        }),
    webpack: !isTurbopack
      ? constructWebpackConfigFunction(incomingUserNextConfigObject, userSentryOptions, releaseName, routeManifest)
      : undefined,
    ...(isTurbopackSupported && isTurbopack
      ? {
          turbopack: constructTurbopackConfig({
            userNextConfig: incomingUserNextConfigObject,
            routeManifest,
          }),
        }
      : {}),
  };' --new_str '  const finalConfig: NextConfigObject = {
    ...incomingUserNextConfigObject,
    ...(nextMajor && nextMajor >= 15
      ? {
          serverExternalPackages: [
            ...(incomingUserNextConfigObject.serverExternalPackages || []),
            ...DEFAULT_SERVER_EXTERNAL_PACKAGES,
          ],
        }
      : {
          experimental: {
            ...incomingUserNextConfigObject.experimental,
            serverComponentsExternalPackages: [
              ...(incomingUserNextConfigObject.experimental?.serverComponentsExternalPackages || []),
              ...DEFAULT_SERVER_EXTERNAL_PACKAGES,
            ],
          },
        }),
    ...(isTurbopackSupported && isTurbopack
      ? {
          turbopack: constructTurbopackConfig({
            userNextConfig: incomingUserNextConfigObject,
            routeManifest,
          }),
        }
      : {}),
  };

  // Only configure webpack if we'"'"'re not using Turbopack
  // If we'"'"'re using Turbopack, we should not set the webpack property at all
  // to avoid Next.js warnings about "Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not"
  if (!isTurbopack) {
    finalConfig.webpack = constructWebpackConfigFunction(
      incomingUserNextConfigObject,

      releaseName,

   325	  // If we're using Turbopack, we should not set the webpack property at all
   326	  // to avoid Next.js warnings about "Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not"
   327	  if (!isTurbopack) {
   328	    finalConfig.webpack = constructWebpackConfigFunction(
   329	      incomingUserNextConfigObject,
   330	      userSentryOptions,
   331	      releaseName,
   332	      routeManifest,
   333	    );
   334	  }
   335	
   336	  return finalConfig;
   337	}

  parseSemver: (version) => {
    // Parse version like "15.3.0"
    const match = version.match(/(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)/);
    if (match) {
      return {
        major: parseInt(match[1], 10),
        minor: parseInt(match[2], 10),

// Create a mock config function based on the fixed logic
function withSentryConfig(nextConfig = {}, sentryBuildOptions = {}) {
  const castNextConfig = nextConfig;

  const isTurbopack = process.env.TURBOPACK;
  const nextJsVersion = getNextjsVersion();
  
  // Simplified version check

  if (nextJsVersion) {

}

// Test the function
console.log('"'"'Testing Sentry configuration with Turbopack enabled...\n'"'"');

const nextConfig = {
  reactStrictMode: true,
  swcMinify: true,
};

const sentryConfig = withSentryConfig(nextConfig, {
  org: '"'"'test-org'"'"',
  project: '"'"'test-project'"'"',
});

console.log('"'"'Generated configuration:'"'"', JSON.stringify({
  hasWebpack: '"'"'webpack'"'"' in sentryConfig,
  hasTurbopack: '"'"'turbopack'"'"' in sentryConfig,
  configKeys: Object.keys(sentryConfig)
}, null, 2));

if ('"'"'webpack'"'"' in sentryConfig) {
  console.log('"'"'\n❌ FAILED: webpack property is present in configuration'"'"');
  console.log('"'"'   This will cause Next.js 15.3 to show the warning: "Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not"'"'"');
  process.exit(1);
} else {
  console.log('"'"'\n✅ SUCCESS: webpack property is NOT present in configuration'"'"');
  console.log('"'"'   Next.js 15.3 will not show the warning about Webpack being configured'"'"');
}

// Also test without Turbopack to ensure webpack is present
console.log('"'"'\n\nTesting Sentry configuration with Turbopack DISABLED...\n'"'"');
delete process.env.TURBOPACK;

const sentryConfigWithoutTurbopack = withSentryConfig(nextConfig, {
  org: '"'"'test-org'"'"',
  project: '"'"'test-project'"'"',
});

console.log('"'"'Generated configuration (no Turbopack):'"'"', JSON.stringify({
  hasWebpack: '"'"'webpack'"'"' in sentryConfigWithoutTurbopack,
  hasTurbopack: '"'"'turbopack'"'"' in sentryConfigWithoutTurbopack,
  configKeys: Object.keys(sentryConfigWithoutTurbopack)
}, null, 2));

if ('"'"'webpack'"'"' in sentryConfigWithoutTurbopack) {
  console.log('"'"'\n✅ SUCCESS: webpack property is present when Turbopack is not enabled'"'"');
} else {
  console.log('"'"'\n❌ FAILED: webpack property should be present when Turbopack is disabled'"'"');
  process.exit(1);
}

console.log('"'"'\n✅ All tests passed! The fix correctly handles Turbopack configuration.'"'"');'

    console.log('"'"'  ✅ SUCCESS: turbopack property is present'"'"');

// This simulates what happens when Next.js processes the configuration

console.log('"'"'=== Integration Test: Next.js 15.3 + Sentry Turbopack Warning Fix ===\n'"'"');

// Mock Next.js configuration processing
function simulateNextJsConfigProcessing(config) {
  const warnings = [];
  
  // Check for the specific warning condition
  if ('"'"'webpack'"'"' in config && config.turbopack !== undefined) {
    warnings.push('"'"'⚠ Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not, which may cause problems.'"'"');
  }
  
  if ('"'"'turbopack'"'"' in config && config.webpack !== undefined) {
    warnings.push('"'"'⚠ Both Webpack and Turbopack configurations are present. This may cause conflicts.'"'"');
  }
  
  return warnings;
}

console.log('"'"'Scenario 1: Turbopack enabled with Sentry config (Fixed behavior)'"'"');
console.log('"'"'------------------------------------------------------------------------\n'"'"');

process.env.TURBOPACK = '"'"'1'"'"';
const Module = require('"'"'module'"'"');
const originalRequire = Module.prototype.require;

// Mock the required modules to simulate a supported Next.js version
Module.prototype.require = function(id) {
  if (id === '"'"'fs'"'"') {
    const fs = originalRequire(id);
    // Mock realpathSync to return a path indicating Next.js 15.3.0
    const originalRealpathSync = fs.realpathSync;
    fs.realpathSync = (path) => {
      if (path.includes('"'"'next/dist'"'"')) {
        return '"'"'/usr/local/lib/node_modules/next/dist'"'"';
      }
      return originalRealpathSync(path);
    };
    return fs;
  }
  return originalRequire.apply(this, arguments);
};

const { withSentryConfig } = require('"'"'./packages/nextjs/build/cjs/config/withSentryConfig'"'"');

// Create a mock Next.js configuration
const userConfig = {
  reactStrictMode: true,
  experimental: {
    instrumentationHook: true,
  },
};

// Apply Sentry configuration
const sentryConfig = withSentryConfig(userConfig, {
  org: '"'"'test-org'"'"',
  project: '"'"'test-project'"'"',
});

console.log('"'"'Generated Sentry configuration:'"'"');
console.log(JSON.stringify({
  hasWebpack: '"'"'webpack'"'"' in sentryConfig,
  hasTurbopack: '"'"'turbopack'"'"' in sentryConfig,
  configKeys: Object.keys(sentryConfig)
}, null, 2));

// Simulate Next.js processing
const warnings = simulateNextJsConfigProcessing(sentryConfig);

if (warnings.length === 0) {
  console.log('"'"'\n✅ SUCCESS: No warnings generated by Next.js!'"'"');
} else {
  console.log('"'"'\n❌ FAILED: Next.js generated warnings:'"'"');
  warnings.forEach(warning => console.log(`   - ${warning}`));
}

Module.prototype.require = originalRequire;

console.log('"'"'\n\nScenario 2: Turbopack disabled (Normal Webpack build)'"'"');
console.log('"'"'-----------------------------------------------------\n'"'"');

delete process.env.TURBOPACK;

// Apply Sentry configuration without Turbopack
const sentryConfigNoTurbo = withSentryConfig(userConfig, {
  org: '"'"'test-org'"'"', 
  project: '"'"'test-project'"'"',
});

console.log('"'"'Generated Sentry configuration (no Turbopack):'"'"');
console.log(JSON.stringify({
  hasWebpack: '"'"'webpack'"'"' in sentryConfigNoTurbo,
  hasTurbopack: '"'"'turbopack'"'"' in sentryConfigNoTurbo,
  configKeys: Object.keys(sentryConfigNoTurbo)
}, null, 2));

// Simulate Next.js processing
const warningsNoTurbo = simulateNextJsConfigProcessing(sentryConfigNoTurbo);

if (warningsNoTurbo.length === 0) {
  console.log('"'"'\n✅ SUCCESS: No warnings generated by Next.js!'"'"');
} else {
  console.log('"'"'\n⚠ Warnings generated by Next.js (expected for Webpack-only builds):'"'"');
  warningsNoTurbo.forEach(warning => console.log(`   - ${warning}`));
}

console.log('"'"'\n\nScenario 3: Original problematic behavior (Before fix)'"'"');
console.log('"'"'----------------------------------------------------------\n'"'"');

// Simulate what would happen before our fix
const problematicConfig = {
  ...userConfig,
  webpack: () => ({/* webpack config */}),
  turbopack: { rules: {} },
};

console.log('"'"'Original problematic configuration:'"'"');
console.log(JSON.stringify({
  hasWebpack: '"'"'webpack'"'"' in problematicConfig,
  hasTurbopack: '"'"'turbopack'"'"' in problematicConfig,
}, null, 2));

const warningsOriginal = simulateNextJsConfigProcessing(problematicConfig);

if (warningsOriginal.length > 0) {
  console.log('"'"'\n✅ This demonstrates the original problem that was fixed:'"'"');
  warningsOriginal.forEach(warning => console.log(`   - ${warning}`));
}

console.log('"'"'\n=== TEST SUMMARY ==='"'"');
console.log('"'"'✅ The fix successfully prevents the Turbopack warning by:'"'"');
console.log('"'"'   - NOT including the webpack property when TURBOPACK=1'"'"');
console.log('"'"'   - Including turbopack configuration when supported'"'"');
console.log('"'"'   - This avoids the "Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not" warning'"'"');
console.log('"'"'\n✅ The fix maintains backward compatibility:'"'"');
console.log('"'"'   - Normal Webpack builds continue to work as expected'"'"');

  console.log(`Test: ${testCase.name}`);
  
  if (testCase.value !== undefined) {
    process.env.TURBOPACK = testCase.value;
  } else {
    delete process.env.TURBOPACK;
  }

    reactStrictMode: true,
  };

  } else {

    allPassed = false;
  }

+  { name: 'TURBOPACK=true (truthy)', value: 'true' },
+  { name: 'TURBOPACK=0 (falsy)', value: '0' },
+  { name: 'TURBOPACK=false (falsy)', value: 'false' },
+  { name: 'TURBOPACK=undefined (not set)', value: undefined },
+];
+
+const { withSentryConfig } = require('./packages/nextjs/build/cjs/config/withSentryConfig');
+
+let allPassed = true;
+
+testCases.forEach(testCase => {
+  console.log(`Test: ${testCase.name}`);
+  
+  if (testCase.value !== undefined) {
+    process.env.TURBOPACK = testCase.value;
+  } else {
+    delete process.env.TURBOPACK;
+  }
+  
+  const mockNextConfig = {
+    reactStrictMode: true,
+  };
+
+  const sentryConfig = withSentryConfig(mockNextConfig, {
+    org: 'test-org',
+    project: 'test-project',
+  });
+  
+  const hasWebpack = 'webpack' in sentryConfig;
+  
+  // Webpack should NOT be present when TURBOPACK is truthy
+  const shouldHaveWebpack = !testCase.value || testCase.value === '0' || testCase.value === 'false' || testCase.value === '';
+  
+  if (hasWebpack === shouldHaveWebpack) {
+    console.log(`  ✅ PASSED: hasWebpack = ${hasWebpack} (expected: ${shouldHaveWebpack})`);
+  } else {
+    console.log(`  ❌ FAILED: hasWebpack = ${hasWebpack} (expected: ${shouldHaveWebpack})`);
+    allPassed = false;
+  }
+  
+  console.log('');

+const hasWebpackAfterMerge = 'webpack' in sentryConfigWithWebpack;

+// Even if user provides webpack config, it should be removed when TURBOPACK=1

+  console.log('  ✅ PASSED: User webpack config correctly removed when TURBOPACK=1');

+// Test script to verify the fix for Next.js 15.3 Turbopack warning
+
+// Simulate the environment where Turbopack is enabled
+process.env.TURBOPACK = '1';
+
+// Mock the modules that would be required
+const mockCore = {
+  isThenable: (val) => typeof val?.then === 'function',
+  parseSemver: (version) => {
+    // Parse version like "15.3.0"
+    const match = version.match(/(\d+)\.(\d+)\.(\d+)/);
+    if (match) {
+      return {
+        major: parseInt(match[1], 10),
+        minor: parseInt(match[2], 10),
+        patch: parseInt(match[3], 10),
+        prerelease: undefined
+      };
+    }
+    return { major: undefined, minor: undefined, patch: undefined, prerelease: undefined };
+  }
+};
+
+const mockNode = {
+  getSentryRelease: () => undefined
+};
+
+// Mock path and fs functions
+const mockFs = {
+  existsSync: () => false,
+  readFileSync: () => ''
+};
+
+const mockPath = {
+  resolve: (...args) => args.join('/'),
+  join: (...args) => args.join('/')
+};
+
+// Mock child_process
+const mockChildProcess = {
+  execSync: () => Buffer.from('mock-git-commit')
+};
+
+// Set up the global object with mocks
+global.require = (modulePath) => {
+  if (modulePath === '@sentry/core') return mockCore;
+  if (modulePath === '@sentry/node') return mockNode;
+  if (modulePath === 'fs') return mockFs;
+  if (modulePath === 'path') return mockPath;
+  if (modulePath === 'child_process') return mockChildProcess;
+  throw new Error(`Cannot find module '${modulePath}'`);
+};
+
+// Mock utilities
+function getNextjsVersion() {
+  return '15.3.0';
+}
+
+function getInstrumentationClientFileContents() {
+  return undefined;
+}

+function setUpTunnelRewriteRules() {}
+function setUpBuildTimeVariables() {}
+function constructWebpackConfigFunction() {
+  return () => ({/* mock webpack config */});
+}
+function constructTurbopackConfig() {
+  return { rules: { /* mock turbopack config */ } };
+}
+
+// Create a mock config function based on the fixed logic
+function withSentryConfig(nextConfig = {}, sentryBuildOptions = {}) {
+  const castNextConfig = nextConfig;
+  
+  // Simplified logic for testing
+  const isTurbopack = process.env.TURBOPACK;
+  const nextJsVersion = getNextjsVersion();
+  
+  // Simplified version check
+  let isTurbopackSupported = false;
+  if (nextJsVersion) {
+    const { major, minor, patch, prerelease } = mockCore.parseSemver(nextJsVersion);
+    isTurbopackSupported = major !== undefined && minor !== undefined && patch !== undefined && 
+      (major > 15 || (major === 15 && minor > 3) || 
+       (major === 15 && minor === 3 && patch === 0 && prerelease === undefined) || 
+       (major === 15 && minor === 3 && patch > 0));
+  }
+  
+  const finalConfig = {
+    ...castNextConfig,
+    ...(isTurbopackSupported && isTurbopack
+      ? { turbopack: constructTurbopackConfig() }
+      : {}),
+  };
+
+  // ONLY configure webpack if we're NOT using Turbopack
+  if (!isTurbopack) {
+    finalConfig.webpack = constructWebpackConfigFunction();
+  }
+
+  return finalConfig;
+}

+  swcMinify: true,
+};

+  org: 'test-org',
+  project: 'test-project',
+});

+// Integration test to verify the complete fix
+// This simulates what happens when Next.js processes the configuration
+
+console.log('=== Integration Test: Next.js 15.3 + Sentry Turbopack Warning Fix ===\n');
+
+// Mock Next.js configuration processing
+function simulateNextJsConfigProcessing(config) {
+  const warnings = [];
+  
+  // Check for the specific warning condition
+  if ('webpack' in config && config.turbopack !== undefined) {
+    warnings.push('⚠ Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not, which may cause problems.');
+  }
+  
+  if ('turbopack' in config && config.webpack !== undefined) {
+    warnings.push('⚠ Both Webpack and Turbopack configurations are present. This may cause conflicts.');
+  }
+  
+  return warnings;
+}
+
+console.log('Scenario 1: Turbopack enabled with Sentry config (Fixed behavior)');
+console.log('------------------------------------------------------------------------\n');
+
+process.env.TURBOPACK = '1';
+const Module = require('module');
+const originalRequire = Module.prototype.require;
+
+// Mock the required modules to simulate a supported Next.js version
+Module.prototype.require = function(id) {
+  if (id === 'fs') {
+    const fs = originalRequire(id);
+    // Mock realpathSync to return a path indicating Next.js 15.3.0
+    const originalRealpathSync = fs.realpathSync;
+    fs.realpathSync = (path) => {
+      if (path.includes('next/dist')) {
+        return '/usr/local/lib/node_modules/next/dist';
+      }
+      return originalRealpathSync(path);
+    };
+    return fs;
+  }
+  return originalRequire.apply(this, arguments);
+};
+
+const { withSentryConfig } = require('./packages/nextjs/build/cjs/config/withSentryConfig');
+
+// Create a mock Next.js configuration
+const userConfig = {
+  reactStrictMode: true,
+  experimental: {
+    instrumentationHook: true,
+  },
+};
+
+// Apply Sentry configuration
+const sentryConfig = withSentryConfig(userConfig, {
+  org: 'test-org',
+  project: 'test-project',
+});
+
+console.log('Generated Sentry configuration:');
+console.log(JSON.stringify({
+  hasWebpack: 'webpack' in sentryConfig,
+  hasTurbopack: 'turbopack' in sentryConfig,
+  configKeys: Object.keys(sentryConfig)
+}, null, 2));
+
+// Simulate Next.js processing
+const warnings = simulateNextJsConfigProcessing(sentryConfig);
+
+if (warnings.length === 0) {
+  console.log('\n✅ SUCCESS: No warnings generated by Next.js!');
+} else {
+  console.log('\n❌ FAILED: Next.js generated warnings:');
+  warnings.forEach(warning => console.log(`   - ${warning}`));
+}
+
+Module.prototype.require = originalRequire;
+
+console.log('\n\nScenario 2: Turbopack disabled (Normal Webpack build)');
+console.log('-----------------------------------------------------\n');
+
+delete process.env.TURBOPACK;
+
+// Apply Sentry configuration without Turbopack

+  configKeys: Object.keys(sentryConfigNoTurbo)
+}, null, 2));
+
+// Simulate Next.js processing
+const warningsNoTurbo = simulateNextJsConfigProcessing(sentryConfigNoTurbo);
+
+if (warningsNoTurbo.length === 0) {
+  console.log('\n✅ SUCCESS: No warnings generated by Next.js!');
+} else {
+  console.log('\n⚠ Warnings generated by Next.js (expected for Webpack-only builds):');
+  warningsNoTurbo.forEach(warning => console.log(`   - ${warning}`));
+}

+console.log('\n\nScenario 3: Original problematic behavior (Before fix)');
+console.log('----------------------------------------------------------\n');

+  console.log('\n✅ This demonstrates the original problem that was fixed:');
+  warningsOriginal.forEach(warning => console.log(`   - ${warning}`));
+}
+
+console.log('\n=== TEST SUMMARY ===');
+console.log('✅ The fix successfully prevents the Turbopack warning by:');
+console.log('   - NOT including the webpack property when TURBOPACK=1');
+console.log('   - Including turbopack configuration when supported');
+console.log('   - This avoids the "Webpack is configured while Turbopack is not" warning');

+  });
